<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>相应的目标函数值等于</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=35
height=41 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image952.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1569" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>第</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>4</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>步得到一极小可行解</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=208
height=49 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image954.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1570"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>而</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=45 height=22
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image956.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1571"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，且目标函数</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=13 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image958.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1572"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的值等于</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>-</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>15</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>所以所要求的目标函数</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=15
height=16 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image960.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1573" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的值为</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>+</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>15</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>[</span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>改进的单纯形法</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>]&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>单纯形法和改进的单纯形法的主要区别在于单纯形法用消去公式变换单纯形表中的所有元素，而改进的单纯形法只要用同样的公式变换基底</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16
height=16 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image962.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1574" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的逆矩阵</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=27
height=20 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image964.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1575" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的元素，一般来说改进的单纯形法计算量比原单纯形法的计算量小</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>为了便于使用改进的单纯形法，引进两个新变量（称为“多余”变量）</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=41
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image966.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1576" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>和</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=43 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image968.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1577"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>如下：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>将一般的线性规划问题</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>4</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>～</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>6</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>改为等价问题：极大化</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>满足条件</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<sub><img width=41 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image969.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1578"
align=absmiddle></sub>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>7</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span></p>
<pre style='text-align:right;line-height:16.0pt' align=right><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=261 height=112
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image971.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1579"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (</span><span
lang=EN-US>8</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span></pre><pre
style='text-align:right;line-height:16.0pt' align=right><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=152 height=97
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image973.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1580"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(</span><span
lang=EN-US>9</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span></pre>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>并且假设所有的</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=41
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image975.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1581" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>再定义“多余方程”：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=317
height=24 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image977.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1582"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;line-height:16.0pt'><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>其中</span></p>
<pre style='text-align:right;line-height:16.0pt' align=right><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=274 height=107
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image979.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1583"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (</span><span
lang=EN-US>10</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span></pre>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>引进人工变量</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=151
height=24 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image981.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1584" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，命</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=75 height=25
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image983.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1585"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，那末可将改进的问题</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(7)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>～</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(9)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>改写为极大化</span></p>
<pre style='text-align:right;line-height:16.0pt' align=right><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=41 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image985.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1586"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (</span><span
lang=EN-US>11</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span></pre>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>满足条件</span></p>
<pre style='text-align:right;line-height:16.0pt' align=right><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=416 height=136
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image987.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1587"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (</span><span
lang=EN-US>12</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span></pre><pre
style='text-align:right;line-height:16.0pt' align=right><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=261 height=155
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image989.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1588"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (</span><span
lang=EN-US>13</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span></pre>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>由</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>10</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>和</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>12</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>有</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=224
height=24 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image991.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1589"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>由于</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=148 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image993.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1590"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，显然</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=43 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image995.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1591"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>不能是正的</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>改进的单纯形法就是通过解改进的线性规划问题</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>11</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>～</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>13</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>来得到一般的线性规划问题</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>4</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>～</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>6</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的解</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>从</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>12</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>中分离出所需要的系数并排成</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=75 height=20
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image997.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1592"></span></sub><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>矩阵如下：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=295
height=195 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image999.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1593"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>将</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=21 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1001.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1594"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的诸列矢量记为</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=145 height=27
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1003.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1595"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>命</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=18 height=16
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1005.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1596"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>为</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=112 height=20
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1007.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1597"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>矩阵</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=260
height=192 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1009.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1598"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=17 height=16
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1011.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1599"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的前</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=13

align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;

font-family:宋体_GB2312'>列表示初始基底</span><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>B</span></i><span

lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>命</span><sub><span

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>将矩阵</span><i><span lang=EN-US

align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;

lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>计算步骤如下：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>第一阶段</span><span lang=EN-US

style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>1</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;

font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=69 height=24

align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，则计算</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span

u1:shapes="_x0000_i1606"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN

  <p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span

  </td>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:24.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>2</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>如果所有的</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=47 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1137.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1671"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，那末</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=43 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1139.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1672"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>达到它的极大值，因此问题</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>7</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>～</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>9</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>不存在可行解</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:24.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>若至少有一 </span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=39
height=24 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1141.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1673" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，则将对应于</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=79
height=36 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1143.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1674"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的变量</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=19 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1145.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1675"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>引入解中</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>若有几个</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=20 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1147.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1676"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>等于极小值，则选择标号</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=13 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1149.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1677"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>最小的</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=20 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1151.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1678"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>3</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>计算</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=473
height=25 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1153.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1679"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>把对应于</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=176
height=45 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1155.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1680" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp; (<sub><img
width=91 height=19 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1157.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1681" align=absmiddle></sub>)</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的变量</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1159.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1682"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>从解中消去</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>若有几个</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1160.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1683"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>对应于极小值，则选择标号</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=10 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1162.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1684"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>最小的</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=17 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1164.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1685"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>4</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>基本可行解中变量的新值由公式</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=100
height=45 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1166.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1686" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp; <sub><img width=47
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1168.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1687" align=absmiddle></sub></span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:7.5pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=56
height=47 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1170.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1688"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>得到</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>矩阵</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=17 height=19
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1172.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1689"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的新元素由变换</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=109
height=48 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1174.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1690" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp; <sub><img width=43
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1176.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1691" align=absmiddle></sub></span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<sub><img width=57 height=48
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1178.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1692"></sub></span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>得到</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>在这个变换下</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=17
height=19 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1180.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1693" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的第</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=37 height=16
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1182.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1694"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>和</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=40 height=16
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1184.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1695"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>列不变</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>重复以上步骤，直到确定没有可行解存在或者</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=68
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1186.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1696" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>如果</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=68 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1187.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1697"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，则进行第二阶段</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>第二阶段</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>在解中无正值的人工变量时：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>1</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>此时</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=68 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1188.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1698"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>计算</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=343
height=25 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1190.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1699" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;(<sub><img width=117
height=24 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1192.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1700" align=absmiddle></sub>)</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>2</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>如果所有的</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=45 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1194.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1701"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，那末</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=41 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1196.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1702"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>达到它的极大值，相应的基本可行解是最优解</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>. <sub><img width=51 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1198.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1703"
align=absmiddle></sub></span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>是要极小化的目标函数的真值</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>如果至少有一个</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=39
height=25 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1200.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1704" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，则将对应于</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=77
height=31 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1202.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1705"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的变量</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=19 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1204.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1706"
align=texttop></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:
宋体_GB2312'>引入解中</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:
宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>若有几个</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=19
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1205.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1707" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>对应于极小值，则选择标号</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=13
height=17 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1207.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1708" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>最小的</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=19 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1209.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1709"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>3</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>计算</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=471
height=25 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1211.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1710"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>把对应于</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=177
height=45 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1213.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1711" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp; (<sub><img
width=89 height=19 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1215.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1712" align=absmiddle></sub>)</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的变量</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1217.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1713"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>从解中消去</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>若有几个</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1219.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1714"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>对应于极小值，则选择标号</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=12 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1221.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1715"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>最小的</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1222.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1716"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>如果所有的</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=45 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1224.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1717"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，那末得到一解其对应的目标函数值可以任意大</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>4</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>变量的新值由公式</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=152
height=93 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1226.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1718"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>得到</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>矩阵</span><i><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>U</span></i><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的新元素由变换</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=219
height=110 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1228.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1719"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>得到</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>重复以上步骤直到确定一个最优解其对应的目标函数值是有限的或者是无限的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>11</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>～</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>13</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的初始解和以上步骤可以按表</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>5</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>所安排的计算步骤实现</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>注意，若矩阵</span><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>A</span></i><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的某一列是单位矢量且其对应的价格系数为零（例如某些松驰矢量），则该矢量可作为基底矢量，这样可以避免使用全人工基底减少迭代次数</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>例</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>2</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>极大化</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=147
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1230.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1720"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>满足条件</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=165
height=75 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1232.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1721"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>和</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
<sub><img width=120 height=25
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1234.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1722"
align=absmiddle></sub></span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>解</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>这里</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=89 height=23
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1236.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1723"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>相应的极小化问题的目标函数为</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=156
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1238.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1724"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>上述问题的全人工基底的改进单纯形法为：极大化满足条件</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=325
height=123 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1240.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1725"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:20.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>第</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>4</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>行的前面四个变量的系数等于原来要极小化的目标函数</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=13 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1242.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1726"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的表达式中的相应的</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1244.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1727"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，第</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>5</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>个方程的变量</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=103
height=24 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1246.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1728" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的系数和方程的右端常数项由公式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>10</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>得到</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>矩阵</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=21 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1248.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1729"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>和</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=17 height=16
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1250.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1730"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>分别为</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=163
height=121 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1252.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1731"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=145

u1:shapes="_x0000_i1732"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>初始表和相继的迭代过程如表</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>6</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:

  <p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><span

  <p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><span
  lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的标号</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=50 valign=top style='width:37.65pt;border-top:solid windowtext 1.5pt;
  border-left:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;border-right:solid windowtext 1.0pt;

  lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:200%'>0&nbsp; 0</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:200%'><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:200%'>0&nbsp; 0</span></p>
  </td>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>[</span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>拉格朗日乘数法</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>]&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>（见第五章§</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>3</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，十）将条件极值问题化为无条件极值问题后可以利用§</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>2</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>和§</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>3</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>无条件极值问题的解法求解</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>[</span><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>惩罚函数法（</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>SUMT</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>方法）</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>]</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=15 height=20
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1353.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1781"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>外点法（</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>SUMT</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>方法之一）</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp; </span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>考虑一般形式的条件极值问题</span></p>
<pre style='text-align:right;line-height:16.0pt' align=right><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=64 height=29
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1355.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1782"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (</span><span
lang=EN-US>14</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span></pre>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>其中</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=247
height=27 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1357.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1783"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>而</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=184 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1359.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1784"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>为定义在</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=23 height=20
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1360.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1785"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>上的连续函数</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>其迭代程序如下：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>1</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>选取</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=52 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1362.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1786"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>（例如取</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=51 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1364.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1787"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>），预先给定的允许误差为</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=37 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1366.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1788"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，令</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=37 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1368.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1789"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>2</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>求无条件极值问题的最优解</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=92 height=25
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1370.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1790"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=201
height=33 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1372.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1791"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>其中</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=284
height=45 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1374.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1792"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>3</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>若存在某</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=76 height=20
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1376.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1793"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，满足</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=95
height=25 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1378.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1794"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>则取</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=77 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1380.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1795"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>（例如</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=143 height=25
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1382.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1796"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>或</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>5</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>），令</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=60
height=19 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1384.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1797" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，进行</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>2</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>；否则就得到条件极值问题</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>14</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的最优解的近似解</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=92
height=25 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1386.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1798" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=17 height=20
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1388.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1799"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>内点法（</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>SUMT</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>方法之二）</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp; </span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>考虑一般形式的条件极值问题</span></p>
<pre style='text-align:right;line-height:16.0pt' align=right><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=65 height=29
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1390.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1800"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <sub><img
width=61 height=24 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1392.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1801" align=absmiddle></sub>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(</span><span
lang=EN-US>15</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span></pre>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>其中</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=251
height=27 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1394.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1802"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>且</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=248
height=27 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1396.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1803"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(<sub><img width=13 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1398.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1804"
align=absmiddle></sub></span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>表示空集</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，而</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=197 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1400.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1805"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>为定义在</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=16
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1402.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1806"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>上的具有一阶连续偏导数的函数，其迭代程序如下：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>1</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>选取</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=40 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1404.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1807"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>（例如取</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=39 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1406.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1808"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>），预先给定的允许误差为</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=37 height=17
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1408.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1809"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>2</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>求</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=16
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1410.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1810"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的内点</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=56 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1412.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1811"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，令</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=37 height=19
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1414.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1812"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>3</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>以</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=73 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1416.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1813"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>作为初始点，对</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=56 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1418.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1814"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>在保持可行性的情况下，使用求解无条件极值问题的方法求解：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=225
height=33 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1420.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1815"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>其中</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=189
height=47 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1422.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1816"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>或</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=211
height=45 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1424.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1817"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>4</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>当取</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=189 height=47
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1426.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1818"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>时，检验是否满足判别准则：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=111
height=47 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1428.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1819"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>而当取</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=211 height=45
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1430.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1820"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>时，检验是否满足判别准则：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=52
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1432.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1821"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>若满足判别准则，则得到条件极值问题</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>15</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)</span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的最优解的近似解</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=29 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1434.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1822"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>；否则，取</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=79 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1436.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1823"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>（例如</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=116 height=41
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1438.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1824"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>或</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>5</span><span
lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>），令</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=60
height=19 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1440.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1825" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，进行</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>3</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>).</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>附：内点求法</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>设</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=213
height=27 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1442.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1826"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=221
height=27 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1444.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1827"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>其中</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=136 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1446.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1828"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>是定义在集合</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=16 height=16
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1448.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1829"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>上的连续函数</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>所谓求内点就是求出一点</span><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=48
height=21 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1450.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1830" align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，其迭代程序如下：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>1</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>任取一点 </span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=64 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1452.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1831"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，及数</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=40 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1454.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1832"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>（例如</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=39 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1456.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1833"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>），令</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=40 height=19
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1458.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1834"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>2</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>求出集合</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=21 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1460.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1835"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>及</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=19 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1462.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1836"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>：</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=221
height=29 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1464.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1837"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=216
height=29 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1466.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1838"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>3</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>若</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=48 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1468.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1839"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，则得到内点</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=91 height=22
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1470.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1840"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，否则，进行</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(4).</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'>4</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>)&nbsp; </span><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>在保持对集合</span><sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=21 height=21
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1472.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1841"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>的可行性的情况下极小化</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=51 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1474.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1842"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>，即</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=77
height=35 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1476.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1843"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>其中</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=172
height=27 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1478.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1844"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=171
height=27 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1480.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1845"></span></sub></p>
<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center;line-height:16.0pt'><sub><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=241
height=49 src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1482.gif"
u1:shapes="_x0000_i1846"></span></sub><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; (<sub><img width=51 height=24
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1484.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1847"></sub>)</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:16.0pt'><span lang=ZH-CN
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>设</span><sub><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'><img width=100 height=25
src="res/17e9d95da129bdd93c34fb6cc6aaaa52_5909_files/image1486.gif" u1:shapes="_x0000_i1848"
align=absmiddle></span></sub><span lang=ZH-CN style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体_GB2312'>为上述问题的最优解的近似解</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>.</span></p>
<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体_GB2312'>(</span><span
